# Census pre-pass — assistive verification worklist (deep-fetched + adversarially hardened)

_Machine 6-point pre-check vs fetched source text → fuller re-fetch of truncation/thin-affected events → adversarial refute pass over every stamp-clean. NOT a verification stamp; the `verified_by:kara` decision stays Kara's. Integrity rule preserved throughout._

**492 events.** Final recommended actions:

- 90 — **stamp-clean**
- 107 — **add-second-source**
- 170 — **fix-then-stamp**
- 78 — **downgrade-confidence**
- 47 — **needs-human-judgment**

**90 events are adversarially-confirmed stamp-clean** — passed the pre-pass AND a skeptic that tried to refute them. This is your high-confidence fast-stamp set.


## How to use this
1. Stamp the **stamp-clean** set first (review each, paste the `qc:` block). 2. Work **downgrade-confidence** (mostly attested→strongly_inferred where the source doesn't name the goal). 3. **add-second-source** (the outlet to add is named per event). 4. **fix-then-stamp** / **needs-human-judgment** last.


---
## stamp-clean (90)

### `2007-01/olympic-games-stuxnet`  _(prepass high ✓✓ refute-confirmed)_
- draft note: Clean P4 load-bearing case. Two secondary sources fetched (Sanger NYT via wayback + Symantec Dossier) plus two book citations (Sanger, Zetter) unfetched-by-design. Event, attribution (US+Israel, caveated as journalism), targets, and three honestly-inferred doctrine links all hold. No second source needed; book citations already provide corroboration depth.
- event_support: supported — NYT/Sanger (wayback) + Symantec Dossier strongly support the core: Sanger — 'code-named Olympic Games', 'developed by the United States and Israel', worm 'escape' summer 2010, 'temporarily took out nearly 1,000 of the 5,000 centrifuges.' Symantec Dossier confirms technical claims: four unpatched Microsoft vulnerabilities, removable-drive self-replication (LNK), Windows + first-ever PLC rootkit, two compromised digital certificates, Siemens PLC sabotage. start_date 2007-01-01 (program inception under Bush) is consistent with 'begun in the Bush administration'; disclosure 2010-06-17 fits 2010 discovery.
- attribution: supported — Sanger names US+Israel explicitly ('developed by the United States and Israel'). actor_id us/olympic-games-team with attributing_org 'David Sanger/NYT (multi-source journalism)' at high confidence; auspex 'concur-with-caveat' appropriate — source notes the program 'remains highly classified' and forensic investigations 'came to no conclusions about who was responsible,' i.e., journalism not official confirmation. The summary's own v0 schema-gap note about the joint US+Israel nature is handled transparently.
- targets: match — Target orgs/natanz-fuel-enrichment-plant matches: Sanger 'Iran's Natanz plant'; Symantec 'majority of infections... in Iran' targeting ICS/Siemens PLCs.
- doctrine: honest — Three doctrine_links, all strongly_inferred, attesting null. us/title-10-title-50 (perspective null) — reasoning transparently notes operation predates NSPM-13 and is tagged as closest extant doctrine. il/begin-doctrine and il/counter-iran-posture both perspective:'attacker-rationale', null attesting — reasoning explicitly states Israeli authorship 'never officially attested by Israel,' so inference framing with null attesting is correct. No overclaim; perspectives appropriate.
